\"\"\"Check if path is a valid path.\n   369→\n   370→    Args:\n   371→        pathstr: The path as string.\n   372→        cwd: The current working directory, or None.\n   373→        relative: Valid segments are:\n   562→                  'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'.\n   563→                  Default: {'path', 'query'}\n   564→\n   565→    Return:\n   566→        The new url with the number incremented/decremented.\n   567→\n   568→    Raises IncDecError if the url contains no number.\n   569→    \"\"\"\n   570→    if not url.isValid():\n   571→        raise InvalidUrlError(url)\n   572→\n   573→    if segments is None:\n   574→        segments = {'path', 'query'}\n   575→    valid_segments = {'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'}\n   576→    if segments - valid_segments:\n   577→        extra_elements = segments - valid_segments\n   578→        raise IncDecError(\"Invalid segments: {}\".format(\n   579→            ', '.join(extra_elements)), url)\n   580→\n   581→    # I found the `incdec_number` function at line 554. Let me analyze it to understand the bug:\n\nThe function `incdec_number` at line 554-605 seems to be the one that handles URL number increment/decrement. The key issue is at line 598:\n\n```python\nmatch = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)', getter())\n```\n\nThis is using `getter()` which gets the URL component (host, path, query, etc.) - but these might be encoded! The issue is:\n\n1. **Encoded sequences are corrupted**: When a URL segment contains something like `%3A5` (percent-encoded colon followed by 5), the regex will match:\n   - Group 1: `%3` (everything up to the last digit)\n   - Group 2: `` (no leading zeros)\n   - Group 3: `A5` (this is treated as digits!)\n   - Group 4: `` (nothing after)\n\n   Actually, wait. `\\d+` matches only digits 0-9. So `%3A5` wouldn't match the pattern because `A` is not a digit. Let me reconsider...\n\n   Actually looking more carefully at the regex: `r'(.*\\D|^)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)'`\n   - This matches: (any characters ending in a non-digit or start) + (optional zeros) + (one or more digits) + (rest)\n\n   So for `%3A5`:\n   - Group 1: `%3A` (the non-digit part)\n   - Group 2: `` (no leading zeros)\n   - Group 3: `5` (the digits)\n   - Group 4: `` (nothing after)\n\n   This should work correctly for `%3A5`. It would increment to `%3A6`.\n\n   Wait, but the problem statement says it's corrupting the `%3A` part. \n\nThe real issue is that `getter()` returns a decoded version of the URL component, not the encoded version. When calling `url.path()`, Qt returns the decoded path. So if the original path is `/%3A5`, the getter returns the decoded form, and the regex operates on that decoded value instead of the percent-encoded original.\n\nThe problem manifests when we have URLs like `http://localhost/%3A5` where percent-encoded sequences get corrupted during the increment operation. The regex is matching against the decoded path rather than preserving the original encoding, which causes the digit extraction and modification to affect the wrong parts of the string.\n\nFor the decrement validation, there's a logic flaw: the check happens before the subtraction, so a value of 1 with a decrement count of 2 would pass the initial check and produce -1 instead of raising an without\nimporting the full qutebrowser module (to avoid circular imports).\n\nThe tests verify the behavior of the incdec_number function in\nqutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py by testing specific bug scenarios.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nimport re\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtCore import QUrl\n\n\n# Define custom exceptions to match qutebrowser's\nclass InvalidUrlError(ValueError):\n    \"\"\"Error raised if a function got an invalid URL.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, url):\n        self.url = url\n        self.msg = f\"Invalid URL: {url.toString()}\"\n        super().__init__(self.msg)\n\n\nclass IncDecError(Exception):\n    \"\"\"Exception raised by incdec_number on problems.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, msg, url):\n        super().__init__(msg)\n        self.url = url\n        self.msg = msg\n\n    def __str__(self):\n        return '{}: {}'.format(self.msg, self.url.toString())\n\n\ndef _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count):\n    \"\"\"Get an incremented/decremented URL based on a URL match.\"\"\"\n    pre, zeroes, number, post = match.groups()\n    val = int(number)\n    if incdec == 'decrement':\n        if val <= 0:\n            raise IncDecError(\"Can't decrement {}!\".format(val), url)\n        val -= count\n    elif incdec == 'increment':\n        val += count\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(\"Invalid value {} for indec!\".format(incdec))\n    if zeroes:\n        if len(number) < len(str(val)):\n            zeroes = zeroes[1:]\n        elif len(number) > len(str(val)):\n            zeroes += '0'\n\n    return ''.join([pre, zeroes, str(val), post])\n\n\ndef incdec_number(url, incdec, count=1, segments=None):\n    \"\"\"Find a number in the url and increment or decrement it.\n\n    This is a copy of the function from qutebrowser/utils/urlutils.py\n    to test it directly without importing the full module.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not url.isValid():\n        raise InvalidUrlError(url)\n\n    if segments is None:\n        segments = {'path', 'query'}\n    valid_segments = {'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'}\n    if segments - valid_segments:\n        extra_elements = segments - valid_segments\n        raise IncDecError(\"Invalid segments: {}\".format(\n            ', '.join(extra_elements)), url)\n\n    # Make a copy of the QUrl so we don't modify the original\n    url = QUrl(url)\n    # Order as they appear in a URL\n    segment_modifiers = [\n        ('host', url.host, url.setHost),\n        ('port', lambda: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',\n         lambda x: url.setPort(int(x))),\n        ('path', url.path, url.setPath),\n        ('query', url.query, url.setQuery),\n        ('anchor', url.fragment, url.setFragment),\n    ]\n    # We're searching the last number so we walk the url segments backwards\n    for segment, getter, setter in reversed(segment_modifiers):\n        if segment not in segments:\n            continue\n\n        # Get the last number in a string\n        match = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)', getter())\n        if not match:\n            continue\n\n        setter(_get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count))\n
